view.tree
$my_debug $mol_book2
  pages /
    <= Page1 $mol_page
      tools /
        <= Github $mol_link_source
          uri \https://github.com/PavelZubkov/my_debug/
      title @ \1
      body /
        <= Date1 $mol_date
          align \bottom_right
          value_moment?val <=> date1?val $mol_time_moment
    <= Page2 $mol_page
      title @ \2
      body /
        <= Date2 $mol_date
          align \bottom_right
          value_moment?val <=> date2?val $mol_time_moment
    <= Page3 $mol_page
      title @ \3
      body /
        <= Date3 $mol_date
          align \bottom_right
          value_moment?val <=> date3?val $mol_time_moment


view.ts
namespace $.$$ {

  export class $my_debug extends $.$my_debug {

    @ $mol_mem
    date1( next? : $mol_time_moment ) {
      if (next) return next

      const date = new $mol_time_moment().merge({ day: 0, hour: 0, minute: 0, second: 0 })
      return date
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    date2( next? : $mol_time_moment ) {
      if (next) return next

      const date = new $mol_time_moment()
      return date
    }



  }

}

    @ $mol_mem
    user_from(next?: $gd_chess_position | null) { return next ?? null }

    @ $mol_mem
    bot_moving() {
      const model = this.model()
      if (! model.bot_active()) return false
      const move = model.best()[0]
      model.move_add(move)
      this.bot_say(move)
      return true
    }

    @ $mol_action
    user_say(move: $gd_chess_move) {
      // say and wait user move bla-bla
    }

    @ $mol_action
    bot_say(move: $gd_chess_move) {
      // say and wait bot move bla-bla
    }

    override click(pos: $gd_chess_position, e?: Event) {
      e && $mol_wire_sync(e).preventDefault()
      const model = this.model()

      if ( model.bot_active()) return

      const from = this.user_from()
      if (! from) {
        this.user_from(pos)
        return
      }

      const move = { from, to: pos }
      model.move_add(move)
      this.user_say(move)
      this.user_from(null)
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    bot_move_auto() {
      const model = this.model()
      if (this.active_color() !== model.bot_color()) return false

      const move = model.best()[0]
      model.move_add(move)
      this.move_pending(move)

      return false
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    active_color() {
      const model = this.model()
      const color = model.active_color()
      const move = this.move_pending()
      if (move) {
        const is_bot = color === model.bot_color()
        this.say(move, is_bot)
        this.move_pending(null)
      }

      return color
    }

    override auto() {
      this.bot_move_auto()
      this.active_color()
    }

    @ $mol_action
    say(move: $gd_chess_move, is_bot = false) {
      // say and wait bot move bla-bla
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    move_pending(next?: $gd_chess_move | null) {
      return next ?? null
    }

class Component {
  id: string = '';

  static Render<T extends typeof Component>(this: T, props: InstanceType<T>) {
    const instance = new this();
    Object.assign(instance, props);
    return instance.render();
  }

  static get View() {
    return this.Render.bind(this);
  }

  render(): string {
    return `Rendering ${this.id}`;
  }
}

class Button extends Component {
  title() { return "" }
}

    ^
    gd_chess_piece_color <= color \w
  type \p
  icons *$mol_icon
    b <= Bishop $mol_icon_chess_bishop - —Å–ª–æ–Ω
    k <= King $mol_icon_chess_king - –∫–æ—Ä–æ–ª—å

namespace $.$$ {
  export class $gd_chess_piece extends $.$gd_chess_piece {
    override color() {
      return $gd_chess_model.piece_color(this.type()) ?? 'w'
    }

    override path() {
      return this.icons()[this.type().toLowerCase()].path()
    }
    
  }
}
